This policy contains 4 data groups.  The data practices of each group will be explained separately.</p>\n\n\t<h3>Group \"Access log information\"</h3>\n\t<p>We collect the following information:</p>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Click-stream data</li>\n\t\t<li>Search terms</li>\n\t\t<li>Last URI requested by the user</li>\n\t\t<li>User agent information</li>\n\t</ul>\n\n\t<p>This data will be used for the following purposes:</p>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Completion and support of the current activity.</li>\n\t\t<li>Web site and system administration.</li>\n\t\t<li>Research and development.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\n\t<p>This data will be used only by ourselves.</p>\n\t<br>\n\t<p>The following explanation is provided for why this data is collected:</p>\n\t<em class=\"lead\">Our Web server collects access logs containing this information.</em>\n\n\t<h3>Group \"Cookies\"</h3>\n\t<p>We collect the following information:</p>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>HTTP cookies</li>\n\t\t<li>Unique identifiers</li>\n\t</ul>\n\n\t<p>This data will be used for the following purposes:</p>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Research and development.</li>\n\t\t<li>One-time tailoring.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\n\t<p>This data will be used only by ourselves.</p>\n\n\t<p>The following explanation is provided for why this data is collected:</p>\n\t<em class=\"lead\">Cookies are used to track visitors to our site, so we can better understand what portions of our site best serve you. We also use cookies to allow our server to maintain information about the contents of your shopping cart.</em>\n\n\t<h3>Group \"Transaction info (required)\"</h3>\n\t<p>We collect the following information:</p>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Physical contact information</li>\n\t\t<li>Online contact information</li>\n\t\t<li>Purchase information</li>\n\t\t<li>Search terms</li>\n\t\t<li>User's Name</li>\n\t\t<li>Name of User's Employer</li>\n\t\t<li>Transaction history</li>\n\t\t<li>Computer information</li>\n\t</ul>\n\n\t<p>This data will be used for the following purposes:</p>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Completion and support of the current activity.</li>\n\t\t<li>Research and development.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\n\t<p>This data will be used only by ourselves.  In addition, the following types of entities will receive this information:</p>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Delivery services.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\n\t<p>The following explanation is provided for why this data is collected:</p>\n\t<em class=\"lead\">Information we collect in order to process your purchase.</em>\n\n\t<h3>Group \"Transaction info (optional)\"</h3>\n\t<p>We collect the following information:</p>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Name of User's Employer</li>\n\t\t<li>User's Home Contact Information</li>\n\t\t<li>User's Business Contact Information</li>\n\t\t<li>Contact Information for the Organization</li>\n\t\t<li>Organization Name</li>\n\t\t<li>Department or division of organization</li>\n\t</ul>\n\n\t<p>This data will be used for the following purposes:</p>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Contacting visitors for marketing of services or products.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\n\t<p>This data will be used only by ourselves.  In addition, the following types of entities will receive this information:</p>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Delivery services.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\n\t<p>The following explanation is provided for why this data is collected:</p>\n\t<em class=\"lead\">Information we collect in order to process your purchase.</em>\n\n\t<h2>Cookies</h2>\n\t<p>Cookies are a technology which can be used to provide you with tailored information from a Web site. A cookie is an element of data that a Web site can send to your browser, which may then store it on your system. You can set your browser to notify you when you receive a cookie, giving you the chance to decide whether to accept it.</p>\n\t<p>In some cases we may collect cookies from 3rd parties, such as Google or DoubleClick.</p>\n\t<p>You can opt out of DoubleClick's use of cookies by visiting: <a href=\"http://www.doubleclick.com/privacy/dart_adserving.aspx\" target=\"_blank\">DoubleClick opt-out page</a></p>\n\t<p>You can opt out of Google's use of cookies by visiting: <a href=\"http://www.google.com/privacy_ads.html\" target=\"_blank\">Google advertising opt-out page</a></p>\n\t<p>Our site makes use of cookies.  Cookies are used for the following purposes:</p>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>User targeting</li>\n\t\t<li>Research and development</li>\n\t</ul>\n\n\t<h2>Compact Policy Summary</h2>\n\t<p>The compact policy For more information, see the P3P deployment guide at <a href=\"http://www.w3.org/TR/p3pdeployment\">http://www.w3.org/TR/p3pdeployment</a>.</p>\n\t<br>\n\t<h2>Policy Evaluation</h2>\n\t<p>Microsoft Internet Explorer 6 will evaluate this policy's compact policy whenever it is used with a cookie.  The actions IE will take depend on what privacy level the user has selected in their browser (Low, Medium, Medium High, or High; the default is Medium.  In addition, IE will examine whether the cookie's policy is considered satisfactory or unsatisfactory, whether the cookie is a session cookie or a persistent cookie, and whether the cookie is used in a first-party or third-party context.  This section will attempt to evaluate this policy's compact policy against Microsoft's stated behavior for IE6.</p>\n\t<p><b>Note:</b> this evaluation is currently experimental and should not be considered a substitute for testing with a real Web browser.</p>\n\t<p><b>Unsatisfactory policy</b>: this compact policy is considered <em>unsatisfactory</em> according to the rules defined by Internet Explorer 6.  The behavior of Internet Explorer 6 regarding cookies set under this compact policy is as follows:</p>\n\n\n\t\t<table class=\"small table\">\n            <thead>\n\t\t\t    <tr>\n\t\t\t\t    <th width=\"20%\"></th>\n\t\t\t\t    <th><b>First-party usage</b></th>\n\t\t\t\t    <th><b>Third-party usage</b></th>\n\t\t\t    </tr>\n            </thead>\n            <tbody>\n\t\t\t    <tr>\n\t\t\t\t    <td><b>Persistent Cookies</b></td>\n\t\t\t\t    <td>\n\t\t\t\t\t    <ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t    <li><b>Low:</b> Policy satisfactory at this level; cookies will be accepted.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t    <li><b>Medium:</b> Opt-out is not provided for all unsatisfactory purposes and recipients, so the cookie will be <b>downgraded</b> to a session cookie.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t    <li><b>Medium High:</b> No opt-out is provided, so the cookie will be <b>blocked</b>.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t    <li><b>High:</b> Since opt-in is not required, the cookie will be <b>blocked</b>.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t    </ul>\n\t\t\t\t    </td>\n\t\t\t\t    <td>\n\t\t\t\t\t    <ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t    <li><b>Low:</b> Opt-out is not provided for all unsatisfactory purposes and recipients, so the cookie will be <b>downgraded</b> to a session cookie.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t    <li><b>Medium:</b> Opt-out is not provided for all unsatisfactory purposes and recipients, so the cookie will be <b>blocked</b>.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t    <li><b>Medium High:</b> Since opt-in is not required, the cookie will be <b>blocked</b>.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t    <li><b>High:</b> Since opt-in is not required, the cookie will be <b>blocked</b>.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t    </ul>\n\t\t\t\t    </td>\n\t\t\t    </tr>\n\t\t\t    <tr>\n\t\t\t\t    <td><b>Session Cookies</b></td>\n\t\t\t\t    <td>\n\t\t\t\t\t    <ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t    <li><b>Low:</b> Policy satisfactory at this level; cookies will be accepted.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t    <li><b>Medium:</b> Policy satisfactory at this level; cookies will be accepted.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t    <li><b>Medium High:</b> Policy satisfactory at this level; cookies will be accepted.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t    <li><b>High:</b> Since opt-in is not required, the cookie will be <b>blocked</b>.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t    </ul>\n\t\t\t\t    </td>\n\t\t\t\t    <td>\n\t\t\t\t\t    <ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t    <li><b>Low:</b> Policy satisfactory at this level; This policy is placed in the unsatisfactory category, because the following categories of data are associated with this policy's cookies:</p>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Physical contact information is collected.</li>\n\t\t<li>Online contact information is collected.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t<p>In addition, the data is used in the following manner, marking the policy as unsatisfactory:</p>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>The data is used for contacting the user.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t<p>Note that allowing an opt-out will make this policy acceptable under the Low and Medium settings, and under Medium High for first-party cookie usage.
